[27/01/26, 1:59:47 PM] ~ Mayank: • KM Calculation (as per rate card):
Payout = Max of [7 × (Pickup + Drop distance), ₹25]

Example 1: Distance = 3.6 km → 3.6 × 7 = ₹25.2 (greater than ₹25, so ₹25.2 applicable)

Example 2: Distance = 2 km → 2 × 7 = ₹14 (less than ₹25, so ₹25 minimum applicable)

• Retail orders count not showing in Kaptaan app – issue identified and currently being fixed.

• Swiggy orders – customer contact number showing 11 digits
(Extra ‘0’ added as the 3rd digit) – this will be removed; fix in progress.

• Order origin identification (Swiggy / Zomato):
Currently visible only after order acceptance.
Food vs non-food differentiation before acceptance is not possible at the moment.
Order ID and items are sufficient to identify the item

• Payout delays to riders:
Acknowledged being taken up on priority.

• Peak hour surge:
₹5 surge charge already added can start marketing on same grounds on daily basis.

• Apollo orders failed due to stock unavailability:
Payout for such cases will be personally added.

[10/02/26, 1:33:15 PM] ~ Tamil: Hi Nikhil ,
   As discussed earlier, last week we had the potential to achieve a 1K DRR (65+ Logins online ). However, due to low to zero demand during the first half and post 12AM ,  most riders did not show interest in continuing online.
We held the rider pool for nearly three days and had multiple discussions internally, during which we acknowledged the impact. Unfortunately, there was no improvement observed in morning and late-night demand windows, while competitor platforms were seeing better order flow and enabling stronger earning potential for riders.
Over the last three days, demand has started to stabilize, and we have begun gradually pulling riders back online. In parallel, we are working on a revised RC structure focused on ensuring decent earnings for mid-level and high-performing riders. Once this goes live, we are confident it will help drive rapid growth in a short span.
Also FR Candidate is Expected to join on Coming Monday. 

Meanwhile, we request your support in reviewing the current penalty structure. riders are paid ₹25 for a forward base while being penalized ₹50, which is causing disappointment on the ground and leading to rider attrition. [27/02/26, 4:10:37 PM] Amaan Blitz: PD, the issue here is that the payout shown in Kaptaan is in IST, while in Ledger it is in GMT. Because of this time difference, there is a 5.5-hour gap.
Last time a similar case came up, the rider actually received a higher payment compared to what was displayed on Kaptaan. There was no escalation at that time. However, when the excess amount was adjusted the following week, escalations were raised.
So the problem is not that the payment is lower - it’s just a difference in time zones causing the mismatch.
Nikhil bhai had suggested making changes in the query, but that’s not feasible because the query is iterating over the ledger. Any correction would need to be handled from the production side. ‎<This message was edited>

வணக்கம் TEV ரைடர்கள்,

நாளை முதல் ஆர்டர் நேர அட்டவணை:

* காலை 6:00 – மதியம் 12:00 : Instamart ஆர்டர்கள்
* மதியம் 1:00 – மாலை 4:00 : உணவு ஆர்டர்கள்
* மாலை 5:00 – மாலை 7:00 : Instamart ஆர்டர்கள்
* மாலை 7:00 – இரவு 12:00 : உணவு ஆர்டர்கள்

இது தான் ஆர்டர் அமைப்பு. ஆர்டர்கள் தொடர்ந்து வரும், அதனால் “ஆர்டர் இல்லை” என்று குழுவில் கூற வேண்டாம்.

உங்களுக்கு ஆர்டர் வரவில்லை என்றால், Demand Sheet-ல் குறிப்பிடப்பட்ட அருகிலுள்ள பகுதிக்கு செல்லுங்கள். எங்கள் Operations குழு அதை பார்த்து ரோஸ்டர் அமைப்பார்கள்.

மேலும், குழுவில் தேவையற்ற மெசேஜ்கள் அனுப்ப வேண்டாம்.

முக்கியமான கேள்விகள் இருந்தால் Operations குழுவிற்கு நேரடியாக கால் செய்யவும், அவர்கள் உதவி செய்வார்கள்.

அனைத்து ரைடர்களும் மேலே கூறியவற்றை பின்பற்ற வேண்டும்.

நன்றி.


ಹಲೋ TEV ರೈಡರ್ಸ್,

ನಾಳೆಯಿಂದ ಆರ್ಡರ್ ಸಮಯದ ವೇಳಾಪಟ್ಟಿ ಈ ಕೆಳಗಿನಂತಿರುತ್ತದೆ:

* ಬೆಳಗ್ಗೆ 6:00 – ಮಧ್ಯಾಹ್ನ 12:00 : Instamart ಆರ್ಡರ್‌ಗಳು
* ಮಧ್ಯಾಹ್ನ 1:00 – ಸಂಜೆ 4:00 : ಆಹಾರ ಆರ್ಡರ್‌ಗಳು
* ಸಂಜೆ 5:00 – ಸಂಜೆ 7:00 : Instamart ಆರ್ಡರ್‌ಗಳು
* ಸಂಜೆ 7:00 – ರಾತ್ರಿ 12:00 : ಆಹಾರ ಆರ್ಡರ್‌ಗಳು

ಇದು ಆರ್ಡರ್ ವ್ಯವಸ್ಥೆ. ಆರ್ಡರ್‌ಗಳು ನಿರಂತರವಾಗಿ ಬರುತ್ತವೆ, ಆದ್ದರಿಂದ “ಆರ್ಡರ್ ಇಲ್ಲ” ಎಂದು ಗ್ರೂಪ್‌ನಲ್ಲಿ ಹೇಳಬೇಡಿ.

ನಿಮಗೆ ಆರ್ಡರ್ ಸಿಗದಿದ್ದರೆ, Demand Sheet ನಲ್ಲಿ ನೀಡಿರುವ ಹತ್ತಿರದ ಪ್ರದೇಶಕ್ಕೆ ಹೋಗಿ. ನಮ್ಮ Operations ತಂಡ ರೋಸ್ಟರ್ ಅನ್ನು ಅದಕ್ಕೆ ಅನುಗುಣವಾಗಿ ವ್ಯವಸ್ಥೆ ಮಾಡುತ್ತದೆ.

ದಯವಿಟ್ಟು ಗ್ರೂಪ್‌ನಲ್ಲಿ ಅಗತ್ಯವಿಲ್ಲದ ಸಂದೇಶಗಳನ್ನು ಕಳುಹಿಸಬೇಡಿ.

ಯಾವುದೇ ಪ್ರಮುಖ ಪ್ರಶ್ನೆಗಳು ಇದ್ದರೆ Operations ತಂಡಕ್ಕೆ ನೇರವಾಗಿ ಕರೆ ಮಾಡಿ, ಅವರು ನಿಮಗೆ ಸಹಾಯ ಮಾಡುತ್ತಾರೆ.

ಎಲ್ಲ ರೈಡರ್ಸ್ ಮೇಲಿನ ಸೂಚನೆಗಳನ್ನು ಅನುಸರಿಸಲು ವಿನಂತಿ.

ಧನ್ಯವಾದಗಳು.


హాయ్ TEV రైడర్స్,

రేపటి నుండి ఆర్డర్ టైమింగ్ షెడ్యూల్ ఇలా ఉంటుంది:

* ఉదయం 6:00 – మధ్యాహ్నం 12:00 : Instamart ఆర్డర్లు
* మధ్యాహ్నం 1:00 – సాయంత్రం 4:00 : ఫుడ్ ఆర్డర్లు
* సాయంత్రం 5:00 – సాయంత్రం 7:00 : Instamart ఆర్డర్లు
* సాయంత్రం 7:00 – రాత్రి 12:00 : ఫుడ్ ఆర్డర్లు

ఇది ఆర్డర్ నిర్మాణం. ఆర్డర్లు నిరంతరం వస్తాయి, కాబట్టి గ్రూప్‌లో “ఆర్డర్లు లేవు” అని చెప్పవద్దు.

మీకు ఆర్డర్లు రాకపోతే, Demand Sheet లో పేర్కొన్న సమీప ప్రాంతానికి వెళ్లండి. మా Operations టీమ్ దీనిని పరిశీలించి రోస్టర్‌ను సెట్ చేస్తుంది.

దయచేసి గ్రూప్‌లో అనవసరమైన మెసేజ్లు పంపవద్దు.

ఏమైనా ముఖ్యమైన సందేహాలు ఉంటే Operations టీమ్‌కు నేరుగా కాల్ చేయండి, వారు మీకు సహాయం చేస్తారు.

అన్ని రైడర్లు పై సూచనలను తప్పనిసరిగా పాటించాలి.
